اشرف البدایہ شرح اردو ہدایہ جلد چہارم
۱۹۵
كتاب النكاح
منهن و تؤی الیک من تشاء یعنی ان میں سے آپ جس کو چاہیں اپنے سے دور رکھیں اور جس کو چاہیں اپنے نزدیک رکھیں ۔ (بیان القرآن ) اس آیت سے معلوم ہوتا ہے حضور صلى الله عليه وسلم قسم (باری) کے پابند نہیں ہیں۔ چنانچہ حافظ عبد العظیم منذری نے ذکر کیا کہ آپ نے سوده، جویریہ، ام حبیبہ، صفیہ اور میمونہ کو دور رکھا اور عائشہ اور باقی ازواج مطہرات کو اپنے نزدیک رکھا۔ پس جب آپ صلى الله عليه وسلم پر قتم ہی واجب نہیں ہے، تو قرعہ اندازی کیوں کر واجب ہوگی۔ اور قرعہ کا باب استحباب سے ہونا اسلئے بھی ہے کہ شوہر کے سفر کرنے کے وقت عورت کا کوئی حق ہی نہیں ہے۔ چنانچہ اگر شوہر ان میں سے کسی کو اپنے ساتھ سفر میں لے جائے تو اس کو اس کا اختیار ہے۔ اسی طرح یہ بھی اختیار ہے کہ ان میں سے کسی کو اپنے ساتھ سفر میں نہ لے جائے تو اس کو اس کا اختیار ہے۔ اسی طرح یہ بھی اختیار ہے کہ ان میں سے کسی ایک کے ساتھ سفر کرے اور یہ مدت محسوب نہیں ہوگی۔ اگر منکوحات میں سے کسی ایک نے اپنی باری کسی سوتن کو دے دی تو یہ شرعاً جائز ہے۔ دلیل ، حضرت عروہ سے روایت ہے کہ رسول اللہ صلى الله عليه وسلم نے سودہ بنت زمعہ کو طلاق دی جب آپ صلى الله عليه وسلم نماز کیلئے نکلے تو حضرت سودہ نے آپ کا کپڑا پکڑ لیا اور کہنے لگیں کہ بخدا مجھ کو مردوں کی کوئی حاجت نہیں رہی لیکن میری مراد یہ ہے کہ میر احشر آپ صلى الله عليه وسلم کی ازواج میں ہو اور درخواست کی کہ اللہ کے رسول (صلى الله عليه وسلم) آپ (صلى الله عليه وسلم) سودہ سے رجعت فرمالیں۔ اور سودہ اپنی باری کا دن عائشہ کیلئے مقرر کر دے گی۔ اور جس عورت نے اپنی باری کا دن دوسری اپنی سوتن کو دے دیا اس کیلئے جائز ہے کہ وہ اپنے اس حق کو واپس لے لے۔ کیونکہ اس نے ایسا حق ساقط کیا جو ابھی تک واجب نہیں ہوا۔ لہذا وہ ساقط ہی نہیں ہوگا۔ پس یہ رجوع اپنی باری دینے سے رکنا ہوگا نہ کہ کسی ساقط شدہ چیز کو واپس لینا۔ واللہ اعلم بالصواب جمیل احمد سکر وڈھوی

Ashraf al-Bidayah Sharh Urdu Hidayah Volume Four
195
Kitab al-Nikah
"Minhunna wa tu'zi ilayka man tasha'" means from among them you may keep away whom you wish and draw near whom you wish. (Bayan al-Quran) From this verse it is understood that the Prophet (peace be upon him) is not bound by division (qasm). Thus Hafiz Abdul Azim al-Mundhiri mentioned that he kept away Saudah, Juwayriyah, Umm Habibah, Safiyyah, and Maymunah, and kept Aisha and the remaining pure wives near him. So when qasm is not even obligatory upon the Prophet (peace be upon him), how could drawing lots be obligatory? And the chapter of drawing lots being a matter of recommendation is also because at the time of the husband's travel, the wife has no right. So if the husband takes one of them with him on a journey, he has that choice. Similarly, he has the choice not to take any of them with him. Similarly, he has the choice to travel with just one, and that period will not be counted (against her turn). If one of the wives gives her turn to a co-wife, this is legally permissible. The proof: a narration from Urwah that the Messenger of Allah (peace be upon him) divorced Saudah bint Zam'ah. When the Prophet (peace be upon him) went out for prayer, Saudah caught hold of his garment and said: "By Allah, I no longer have any need for men, but my desire is that I be resurrected among your wives." And she requested: "O Messenger of Allah, take me back (ruju'). And Saudah will assign her night to Aisha." And for a woman who gives her night to another co-wife, it is permissible for her to take back that right, because she waived a right that had not yet become obligatory. Therefore it was not waived. Thus this revocation is a matter of refraining from giving her turn, not taking back something already waived. And Allah knows best what is correct. Jamil Ahmad Sakhar Vadhavi. O Allah, forgive the writer, his parents, and whoever contributed to it. besturdubooks.wordpress.com
Source pages p. 196

Commentary
This passage from Ashraf al-Bidayah, the Urdu commentary on Al-Hidayah, addresses two interconnected rulings related to the division of nights (qasm) among co-wives. First, it establishes that the Prophet Muhammad (peace be upon him) was not obligated to maintain equal division of nights among his wives. The author cites the Quranic verse (Surah al-Ahzab 33:51) which grants the Prophet the choice to keep away or draw near any of his wives, indicating that qasm was not wajib upon him. He further supports this with the observation of Hafiz Abdul Azim al-Mundhiri that the Prophet kept some wives at a distance and others close. Consequently, the question of drawing lots (qur'ah) to determine the order of nights does not arise for him. The text then clarifies that the topic of qur'ah in general is a matter of recommendation (istihbab), not obligation. This is supported by the fact that a wife has no specific right to be taken on a journey; the husband may choose any wife to accompany him without counting that time against her turn. The second ruling addresses the permissibility of a wife voluntarily giving her turn to a co-wife. This is declared legally permissible (ja'iz). The proof provided is a hadith from Urwah ibn al-Zubayr regarding Saudah bint Zam'ah. According to the narration, the Prophet divorced Saudah, but when he went out, she stopped him and expressed her desire to remain among his wives in the Hereafter, asking him to take her back. She offered to give her night to Aisha. The Prophet accepted this. The author, following Hanafi legal reasoning, explains that if a woman gives her turn to another, she may later revoke this gift because she waived a right that had not yet become obligatory (since the night had not arrived). Thus, the waiver did not take effect; she is simply refraining from giving the turn, not reclaiming a waived right. This passage demonstrates the Hanafi approach to deriving rulings from the Sunnah and applying the principle of rights not yet vested.

Key Terms
قسم (باری) (qasm/qism (bārī)): Division of nights among co-wives; the equitable distribution of a husband's time among multiple wives.
قرعہ (qur'ah): Drawing lots to determine the order of nights among co-wives.
باری دینا (bārī denā): A wife giving her turn (night) to a co-wife.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
According to the passage, what is the ruling on a wife giving her turn to a co-wife?
A) It is obligatory to do so.
B) It is prohibited (haram).
C) It is permissible (ja'iz), and she may revoke it.
D) It is recommended (mustahabb) but cannot be revoked.

Key Takeaway
The Prophet was exempt from qasm; a wife may give her turn to a co-wife and revoke it before the turn is due.

Nikah — Marriage
intermediate

Quantity of Milk in Fosterage: Hanafi vs Shafi'i
Dispute on minimum milk quantity for fosterage prohibition

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to state the Hanafi position on the minimum quantity of milk for fosterage prohibition and explain why the Shafi'i objection is rejected.

Core Idea
Any amount of breast milk, within the breastfeeding period, establishes the prohibition of marriage — Hanafis reject any minimum number.

This passage presents a classic dispute between the Hanafi and Shafi'i schools on a fundamental issue of family law: does a tiny amount of breast milk create a permanent marriage prohibition? The Hanafi school, relying on the general wording of the Quran, holds that any quantity suffices. We will examine the proofs from both sides and see why the Hanafi position is preferred.

Guided Path
1
State the Hanafi position
What does the Hanafi school hold regarding the quantity of milk required for fosterage prohibition?
The answer: any amount, small or large, within the breastfeeding period.
2
Identify the opponent and their view
Which school objects and what is their position?
Imam al-Shafi'i requires five separate sucklings.
3
Follow the opponent's proof
What dalil does al-Shafi'i cite?
The hadith: 'One suckle or two does not make unlawful, nor one gulp or two.'
4
Analyse the Hanafi response
How does the Hanafi school rebut this?
The hadith is either weak or abrogated by the Quranic general command.
5
Determine the thamarah al-khilaf
What is the practical difference in rulings?
Hanafi: any single instances creates prohibition. Shafi'i: only after five separate sessions.

Source Text

كتاب الرضاع
ترجمہ (یہ) کتاب دودھ پینے پلانے کے بیان میں ہے)
تشریح درضا افتح الراء اصل ہے اور کسر راء کے ساتھ بھی ایک لغت ہے فصیح لغت میں جمع سے ہے۔ اور اہل نجد نے کہا کہ ضرب سے ہے۔ لغت میں رضاعت چھاتی سے دودھ چوسنے کو کہتے ہیں اور شریعت میں رضیع کا آدمیہ کی چھاتی سے دودھ چوسنا وقت مخصوص میں۔ آدمیہ کی چھاتی کی قید لگا کر احتراز ہے حیوان کی چھاتی ہے۔ چنانچہ اگر بکری وغیرہ کا دودھ پی لیا تو اس سے رضاعت ثابت نہیں ہوگی۔ اور وقت مخصوص سے مراد مدت رضاعت ہے۔ اور اس کی تحدید میں اختلاف ہے جس کو آگے بیان کریں گے۔ انشاء اللہ تعالیٰ دودھ کی کتنی مقدار کے ساتھ حرمت رضاعت متعلق ہوتی ہے
قال قليل الرضاع وكثيره سواء اذا حصل في مدة الرضاع يتعلق به التحريم وقال الشافعي لا يثبت التحريم الا بخمس رضعات لقوله عليه السلام لاتحرم المصة ولا المصتان ولا الاملاجته ولا الاملاجتان ولنا قوله تعالى وامها تكم اللاتي ارضعنكم الاية وقوله عليه السلام يحرم من الرضاع ما يحرم من النسب من غير فصل ولان الحرمة و ان كانت لشبهة البعضية الثابتة بنشور العظم وانبات اللحم لكنه امر مبطن فتعلق الحكم بفعل الارضاع ومارواه مردود بالكتاب او منسوخ به وينبغي ان يكون في مدة الرضاع لمانبين ترجمہ فرمایا کہ رضاعت کا قلیل و کثیر برابر ہے۔ جب یہ رضاعت ) مدت رضاعت میں پائی جائے تو اسکے ساتھ تحریم متعلق ہو گی۔ اور کہا امام شافعی نے کہ تحریم نہیں ثابت ہوتی مگر پانچ گھونٹ سے حضور صلى الله عليه وسلم کے فرمان لا تحرم الامصة الحديث كى وجہ سے نہیں حرام کرتا ایک چوسنا اور دو چوسنے اور نہ ایک بار چوسانا اور نہ دو بار چوسانا۔ اور ہماری دلیل باری تعالیٰ کا قول ہے (اور تم پر حرام کی گئیں ) تمہاری وہ مائیں جنہوں نے تم کو دودھ پلایا اور نبی کا قول حرام ہو جاتا ہے رضاعت سے جو حرام ہو جاتا ہے نسب سے بغیر تفصیل کے اور اسلئے کہ حرمت اگر چہ اس شبہ بعضیت کی وجہ سے ہے جو ثابت ہے ہڈی بڑھ جانے اور گوشت اگانے سے ۔ لیکن یہ امر باطن ہے۔ پس حکم متعلق ہوا دودھ پلانے کے فعل کے ساتھ اور وہ حدیث جس کو امام شافعی نے روایت کیا کتاب اللہ سے مردود ہے یا اس سے منسوخ ہے اور مناسب ہے کہ رضاع ( دودھ پینا ) مدت رضاعت میں ہو۔ تشریح دودھ کی مقدار ( جس سے حرمت رضاعت ثابت ہو جائے گی ) میں اختلاف ہے احناف کا مذہب یہ ہے کہ مطلقا دودھ پینا یا پلا نا حرمت رضاعت ثابت کرتا ہے۔ بشرطیکہ مدت رضاعت میں ہو ۔ اسی کے قائل حسن بصری ، سعید بن المسیب ، وکیع ،عبداللہ بن المبارک اور اکثر جمہور فقہاء ہیں۔ حضرت امام شافعی فرماتے ہیں کہ پانچ مرتبہ دودھ پینے سے حرمت رضاعت ثابت ہوگی ۔ بایں معنی کہ بچہ ان میں سے ہر ایک مرتبہ پر اکتفا کرے اور ظاہر الروایۃ میں امام احمد اسی کے قائل ہیں۔ اور امام احمد سے دوسری روایت تین مرتبہ پینے کی ہے۔
Book of Fosterage: This book is about breastfeeding. Explanation: 'Rada' has two pronunciations: with fatha on ra and with kasr on ra; both are a language. The more eloquent language is from the root jama'a (to collect). The people of Najd said it is from daraba. In language, rada'ah means sucking milk from the breast. In Shari'ah, it is the sucking of milk from the breast of a human female by a suckling child within a specific time. The restriction 'human female' excludes animals: if a child drinks milk from a goat etc., fosterage is not established. 'Specific time' refers to the breastfeeding period, the definition of which differs and will be explained later. The commentary states: He (the author) said: The small quantity and the large quantity of fosterage are equal when it occurs within the breastfeeding period; prohibition attaches to it. Al-Shafi'i said: Prohibition is only established by five sucklings, because of his saying, peace be upon him: 'One suckle or two does not make unlawful, nor one gulp or two.' Our evidence is the saying of Allah Most High: 'Your mothers who have suckled you...' and his saying, peace be upon him: 'What is prohibited through fosterage is what is prohibited through lineage' without distinction. And because the prohibition, although due to the resemblance of partiality established by the growth of bone and flesh, is a hidden matter, so the ruling is attached to the act of breastfeeding. And what he (Shafi'i) narrated is rejected by the Book or abrogated by it. And it is necessary that it be within the breastfeeding period. Explanation: There is a difference of opinion regarding the quantity of milk from which the prohibition of fosterage is established. The Hanafis' madhhab is that absolutely drinking or giving milk establishes the prohibition of fosterage, provided it is within the breastfeeding period. This is also the view of Hasan al-Basri, Sa'id ibn al-Musayyib, Waki', 'Abdullah ibn al-Mubarak, and the majority of jurists. Imam al-Shafi'i says that prohibition is established by five milk-drinkings, meaning the child satiates with each one. In the apparent narration (zahir al-riwayah), Imam Ahmad also held this view, and from Imam Ahmad there is another narration of three drinkings.
Source pages p. 198

Commentary
This passage is an inter-madhhab dispute concerning the quantity of breast milk required to establish the prohibition of marriage due to fosterage (rada'). The author begins by defining fosterage linguistically and legally, then presents the Hanafi position: any amount of milk, whether small or large, establishes prohibition as long as it occurs within the breastfeeding period. The Hanafi evidence includes the Quranic verse (4:23) which declares foster mothers as prohibited in marriage, and the hadith 'What is prohibited through fosterage is what is prohibited through lineage,' which indicates no distinction between small and large quantities. The Shafi'i position requires five separate sucklings, based on a hadith stating that one or two sucklings do not make unlawful. The Hanafi response argues that the Shafi'i hadith is either weak and rejected by the Quran or abrogated. The passage then summarizes that the majority of early scholars (including Hasan al-Basri, Sa'id ibn al-Musayyib, etc.) agree with the Hanafi view. Imam Ahmad's position is noted as having two narrations: one requiring five sucklings and another requiring three. The relied-upon Hanafi position is that any quantity suffices, irrespective of number, provided the milk is consumed during the recognized breastfeeding period (usually two years).

Key Terms
رضاع (rada'): In this passage, rada' refers to the act of a child sucking milk from a human female's breast.
قليل وكثير (qalil wa kathir): The small or large quantity of milk consumed by the child.
مدة الرضاع (muddah al-rada'): The recognized period of breastfeeding within which fosterage prohibition applies.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
According to the Hanafi madhhab, how many sucklings are required for fosterage prohibition to take effect?
A) Any amount, regardless of number
B) Five separate sucklings
C) Three separate sucklings
D) At least twenty sucklings

Key Takeaway
The Hanafi school holds that any amount of human breast milk consumed within the breastfeeding period establishes fosterage prohibition, based on the general Quranic verse and rejection of the Shafi'i hadith.
